 def register_pathB_capture() -> None:
@@ -48,6 +58,54 @@ def clear_pathB_capture() -> None:
     _SINK.set(None)
     _ROLE.set(None)
     _RETRIEVAL.set(None)
+    _ROLE_PROVIDER.set(None)
+
+
+def set_role_providers(mapping: dict[str, str]):
+    """I-bug-946 (#932): set the resolved per-role provider mapping for the gate run.
+
+    Called by gate_around_question() AFTER preflight() resolves each role's served provider
+    via OpenRouter's /api/v1/models/<id>/endpoints. Returns a token; pair with
+    reset_role_providers() in try/finally so the mapping never leaks beyond the gate scope.
+    """
+    return _ROLE_PROVIDER.set(mapping)
+
+
+def reset_role_providers(token) -> None:
+    _ROLE_PROVIDER.reset(token)
+
+
+def current_role_provider() -> str | None:
+    """Return the resolved provider for the CURRENT role (read via _ROLE contextvar).
+
+    Returns None if either the gate is off (mapping is None) or the current role has no
+    entry in the mapping. openrouter_client calls this; when None it falls back to its
+    current env-driven path (gate-off mode).
+
+    NOTE: entailment_judge must NOT use this — see get_role_provider() below.
+    """
+    mapping = _ROLE_PROVIDER.get()
+    if mapping is None:
+        return None
+    role = _ROLE.get()
+    if role is None:
+        return None
+    return mapping.get(role)
+
+
+def get_role_provider(role: str) -> str | None:
+    """Explicit-role lookup, NOT keyed off the ambient _ROLE contextvar.
+
+    I-bug-946 (#932) Codex iter-1 diff P1#2: the entailment judge posts the evaluator
+    model but is INVOKED from within the generator's _ROLE scope (provenance verification
+    fires during section generation). Using current_role_provider() would resolve to the
+    generator's provider (Fireworks) for a Gemma post — Fireworks doesn't host Gemma →
+    silent re-route. The judge must pass role="evaluator" explicitly.
+    """
+    mapping = _ROLE_PROVIDER.get()
+    if mapping is None:
+        return None
+    return mapping.get(role)

+# --- I-bug-946 (#932): per-role provider resolution via /api/v1/models/<id>/endpoints ---
+
+class _MockEndpointsResponse:
+    """Mock requests.Response carrying an OpenRouter endpoints payload."""
+    status_code = 200
+    def __init__(self, endpoints: list[dict]) -> None:
+        self._payload = {"data": {"endpoints": endpoints}}
+    def json(self) -> dict:
+        return self._payload
+    def raise_for_status(self) -> None:
+        return None
+
+
+def _patch_endpoints(monkeypatch, endpoints: list[dict]) -> None:
+    import requests
+    monkeypatch.setattr(requests, "get", lambda *a, **k: _MockEndpointsResponse(endpoints))
+
+
+def test_resolve_role_provider_returns_first_in_order_match(monkeypatch) -> None:
+    _patch_endpoints(monkeypatch, [
+        {"provider_name": "Novita", "status": 0},
+        {"provider_name": "DeepInfra", "status": 0},
+    ])
+    # Order prefers fireworks (absent), then novita (present) — must return Novita.
+    assert resolve_role_provider("google/gemma-4-31b-it", ["fireworks", "novita"]) == "Novita"
+
+
+def test_resolve_role_provider_fails_closed_on_no_intersection(monkeypatch) -> None:
+    _patch_endpoints(monkeypatch, [
+        {"provider_name": "Novita", "status": 0},
+        {"provider_name": "DeepInfra", "status": 0},
+    ])
+    with pytest.raises(GateError, match="no intersection"):
+        resolve_role_provider("google/gemma-4-31b-it", ["fireworks"])
+
+
+def test_resolve_role_provider_skips_degraded_endpoints(monkeypatch) -> None:
+    """Codex P2#4: status != 0 means degraded/lower-priority; skip from intersection."""
+    _patch_endpoints(monkeypatch, [
+        {"provider_name": "Fireworks", "status": -5},  # degraded — must skip
+        {"provider_name": "Novita", "status": 0},
+    ])
+    # If fireworks weren't degraded, would return Fireworks. Since it IS degraded, fall to novita.
+    assert resolve_role_provider("any/model", ["fireworks", "novita"]) == "Novita"
+
+
+def test_resolve_role_provider_fails_closed_on_empty_endpoints(monkeypatch) -> None:
+    _patch_endpoints(monkeypatch, [])
+    with pytest.raises(GateError, match="no endpoints"):
+        resolve_role_provider("any/model", ["fireworks"])
+
+
+def test_resolve_role_provider_case_insensitive_with_catalog_spelling(monkeypatch) -> None:
+    """Codex P2#3: order is case-insensitive; pin preserves catalog spelling."""
+    _patch_endpoints(monkeypatch, [
+        {"provider_name": "Novita", "status": 0},
+    ])
+    # User typed 'NOVITA' in env; catalog spelling is 'Novita'. Returned pin keeps catalog case.
+    assert resolve_role_provider("any/model", ["NOVITA"]) == "Novita"
+
+
+def test_resolve_role_provider_treats_missing_status_as_eligible(monkeypatch) -> None:
+    """Some endpoints omit the status field entirely; treat as status==0 (eligible)."""
+    _patch_endpoints(monkeypatch, [
+        {"provider_name": "Fireworks"},  # no status field
+    ])
+    assert resolve_role_provider("any/model", ["fireworks"]) == "Fireworks"
+
+
+def test_preflight_pins_per_role_from_resolution(monkeypatch) -> None:
+    """End-to-end: preflight populates provider_name per role from endpoint resolution."""
+    _full_power_env(monkeypatch)
+    monkeypatch.setenv("OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER", "fireworks,novita")
+    # Pre-injected RolePins so offline=True path skips the resolver entirely; this test
+    # asserts that the role_pin's provider_name flows through to the persisted pin.
+    pins = [
+        RolePin("generator", _GEN_SLUG, "Fireworks", ("provider_name", "model")),
+        RolePin("evaluator", _EVAL_SLUG, "Novita", ("provider_name", "model")),
+    ]
+    pin = preflight([], pins, _SALT, offline=True)
+    assert pin["role_pins"][0]["provider_name"] == "Fireworks"
+    assert pin["role_pins"][1]["provider_name"] == "Novita"
+
+
+def test_preflight_accepts_multi_provider_order(monkeypatch) -> None:
+    """Multi-entry provider_order is now valid (was rejected as non-singleton pre-I-bug-946)."""
+    _full_power_env(monkeypatch)
+    monkeypatch.setenv("OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER", "fireworks,novita")
+    pins = [RolePin("generator", _GEN_SLUG, "Fireworks", ("provider_name", "model"))]
+    pin = preflight([], pins, _SALT, offline=True)
+    assert pin["openrouter_provider_order"] == "fireworks,novita"
+

+def test_preflight_fatal_on_divergent_entailment_model(monkeypatch) -> None:

+def test_preflight_online_resolves_per_role_distinct_providers(monkeypatch) -> None:
+    """Codex iter-1 diff P1#1 regression: online preflight (offline=False) MUST always
+    overwrite provider_name from the resolver, even when RolePin pre-seeds a value. Without
+    this, _role_pins's old env-first-entry seed would silently bypass per-role resolution
+    and pin both roles to the first env provider (the smoke-#15 bug, in a different shape)."""
+    _full_power_env(monkeypatch)
+    monkeypatch.setenv("OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER", "fireworks,novita")
+    # Mock the endpoint resolver to return distinct providers per model: Fireworks for the
+    # generator's model (deepseek-v4-pro) and Novita for the evaluator's (gemma).
+    import requests
+    def _mock_get(url, *args, **kwargs):
+        if "deepseek-v4-pro" in url:
+            return _MockEndpointsResponse([
+                {"provider_name": "Fireworks", "status": 0},
+                {"provider_name": "Novita", "status": 0},
+            ])
+        if "gemma-4-31b-it" in url:
+            return _MockEndpointsResponse([
+                {"provider_name": "Novita", "status": 0},
+                {"provider_name": "DeepInfra", "status": 0},
+            ])
+        # Models endpoint for canonical_slug resolution (I-bug-945) — return a benign list.
+        return _MockEndpointsResponse_models()
+    class _MockEndpointsResponse_models:
+        status_code = 200
+        def __init__(self) -> None: pass
+        def json(self):
+            return {"data": [
+                {"id": _GEN_SLUG, "canonical_slug": _GEN_SLUG + "-x"},
+                {"id": _EVAL_SLUG, "canonical_slug": _EVAL_SLUG + "-y"},
+            ]}
+        def raise_for_status(self) -> None: ...
+    monkeypatch.setattr(requests, "get", _mock_get)
+    # _role_pins() seeds provider_name="" (post-Codex-iter-1 fix); preflight must overwrite.
+    pins = [
+        RolePin("generator", _GEN_SLUG, "", ("provider_name", "model")),
+        RolePin("evaluator", _EVAL_SLUG, "", ("provider_name", "model")),
+    ]
+    pin = preflight([], pins, _SALT, offline=False, reachability_prober=lambda b: True)
+    by_role = {rp["role"]: rp["provider_name"] for rp in pin["role_pins"]}
+    assert by_role["generator"] == "Fireworks"
+    assert by_role["evaluator"] == "Novita"
+

+def test_preflight_fatal_when_only_entailment_model_diverges(monkeypatch) -> None:
+    """Codex iter-1 diff P2#2: if ONLY PG_ENTAILMENT_MODEL is set away from the default and
+    PG_EVALUATOR_MODEL is unset (so the evaluator uses default = gemma-4-31b-it), the gate
+    must STILL fail closed — effective values still differ."""
+    _full_power_env(monkeypatch)

+def test_get_role_provider_explicit_lookup_ignores_ambient_role() -> None:
+    """Codex iter-1 diff P1#2 regression: get_role_provider(role) MUST NOT read ambient _ROLE.
+    The entailment judge fires under _ROLE=='generator' but posts the evaluator model; it
+    must explicitly request the evaluator provider."""
+    from src.polaris_graph.benchmark import pathB_capture as _pb
+    token_rp = _pb.set_role_providers({"generator": "Fireworks", "evaluator": "Novita"})
+    try:
+        with _pb.llm_role("generator"):
+            # Under generator scope, explicit evaluator lookup must still return Novita.
+            assert _pb.get_role_provider("evaluator") == "Novita"
+            # And current_role_provider (ambient-based) returns Fireworks per spec.
+            assert _pb.current_role_provider() == "Fireworks"
+    finally:
+        _pb.reset_role_providers(token_rp)
+
+
+def test_role_provider_contextvar_set_get_reset() -> None:
+    """The pathB_capture ContextVar must roundtrip: set → get-by-role → reset."""
+    from src.polaris_graph.benchmark import pathB_capture as _pb
+    # Outside any role/gate scope, get returns None.
+    assert _pb.current_role_provider() is None
+    token_rp = _pb.set_role_providers({"generator": "Fireworks", "evaluator": "Novita"})
+    try:
+        # Without a role contextvar set, still None (no role to look up).
+        assert _pb.current_role_provider() is None
+        with _pb.llm_role("generator"):
+            assert _pb.current_role_provider() == "Fireworks"
+        with _pb.llm_role("evaluator"):
+            assert _pb.current_role_provider() == "Novita"
+        with _pb.llm_role("unknown_role"):
+            assert _pb.current_role_provider() is None
+    finally:
+        _pb.reset_role_providers(token_rp)
+    assert _pb.current_role_provider() is None

 160: def _role_surrogate(metadata: dict, surrogate_fields: tuple[str, ...] | list) -> str:
 161:     """The served-identity surrogate over the PINNED fields only (Codex P1 — exact pin)."""
 162:     picked = {f: metadata.get(f) for f in surrogate_fields}
 163:     return hashlib.sha256(json.dumps(picked, sort_keys=True).encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()

 166: def preflight(
 167:     control_vars: list[str],
 168:     role_pins: list[RolePin],
 169:     salt: bytes,
 170:     reachability_prober=None,
 171:     source_map: dict[str, list[str]] | None = None,
 172:     roots: list[Path] | None = None,
 173:     offline: bool = False,
 174: ) -> dict:
 175:     """Fatal preflight. Returns the pin record to hash-pin BEFORE the run.
 176: 
 177:     The gate FORCES the complete control surface (Codex iter-2 P1): it always unions the
 178:     retrieval/credential env into `control_vars`, and if `roots` is given it also unions the
 179:     grepped PG_*/OPENROUTER_* surface — so a caller passing `[]` cannot produce an empty config.
 180: 
 181:     Reachability is enforce-by-default for real runs (Codex iter-2 P1): if `offline` is False
 182:     and no prober is given, `real_retrieval_prober` is used (live ping). Tests pass
 183:     `offline=True` to skip the network. `reachability_checked=False` is therefore only
 184:     possible in an explicitly-offline (test) run, never a real run gate.
 185:     """
 186:     # FORCE the complete control surface (retrieval creds always; grepped surface if roots given)
 187:     surface = set(control_vars or [])
 188:     if roots:
 189:         surface |= set(full_control_surface(roots))
 190:     surface |= set(_EXTRA_CONTROL_ENV)
 191:     control_vars = sorted(surface)
 192:     # reachability: enforce-by-default for real runs
 193:     if not offline and reachability_prober is None:
 194:         reachability_prober = real_retrieval_prober
 195:     # 1. fallbacks OFF
 196:     if os.environ.get("OPENROUTER_ALLOW_FALLBACKS", "true").strip().lower() not in ("false", "0", "no"):
 197:         raise GateError("OPENROUTER_ALLOW_FALLBACKS must be false (it defaults TRUE)")
 198:     # 2. provider routing — per-role resolution at preflight (I-bug-946 #932).
 199:     # The env supplies a candidate list (comma-separated). Each role's actual served provider
 200:     # is resolved via OpenRouter's per-model endpoints endpoint and pinned per role. The old
 201:     # "singleton" check rejected multi-provider orders, but disjoint model provider sets
 202:     # require a multi-entry order (e.g. fireworks for deepseek-v4-pro, novita for gemma).
 203:     order = (os.environ.get("OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER") or "").strip()
 204:     provider_order_list = [p.strip() for p in order.split(",") if p.strip()]
 205:     if not provider_order_list:
 206:         raise GateError("OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER must list at least one candidate provider")
 207:     # 3. required retrieval capability — PRESENCE *and* REACHABILITY (Codex P1)
 208:     missing = [c for c in _REQUIRED_RETRIEVAL_CREDS if not os.environ.get(c)]
 209:     if missing:
 210:         raise GateError(f"required retrieval credentials absent — not full-power: {missing}")
 211:     if reachability_prober is not None:
 212:         for cred, backend in _REQUIRED_RETRIEVAL_CREDS_TO_BACKENDS.items():
 213:             if not reachability_prober(backend):
 214:                 raise GateError(f"retrieval backend {backend!r} unreachable/invalid-key — not full-power")
 215:     # 4. each role pin must declare which surrogate fields it PROVED present + a full slug
 216:     for rp in role_pins:
 217:         if not rp.surrogate_fields:
 218:             raise GateError(f"role {rp.role}: no served-identity surrogate fields proven present")
 219:         if "/" not in rp.model_slug:
 220:             raise GateError(f"role {rp.role}: model_slug must be the FULL slug (provider/model), got {rp.model_slug!r}")
 221:         # I-bug-945 (#931): resolve OpenRouter alias to its dated canonical_slug at preflight.
 222:         # The catalog is the single source of truth; fail closed if the alias is unknown.
 223:         # Skipped on offline runs (unit tests pass canonical_slug directly when needed).
 224:         if not offline and rp.canonical_slug is None:
 225:             rp.canonical_slug = resolve_canonical_slug(rp.model_slug)
 226:         # I-bug-946 (#932): resolve per-role provider via /api/v1/models/<id>/endpoints.
 227:         # Codex iter-1 diff P1: online preflight MUST always overwrite provider_name from
 228:         # the resolver, because _role_pins() previously pre-seeded provider_name from the
 229:         # env's first entry (now changed to empty, but the always-overwrite invariant is
 230:         # the defense-in-depth — any future caller passing a non-empty provider_name still
 231:         # gets re-resolved at preflight, so the persisted pin reflects the actual resolution).
 232:         # Offline tests skip the resolver (pre-injected RolePin.provider_name wins).
 233:         if not offline:
 234:             rp.provider_name = resolve_role_provider(rp.model_slug, provider_order_list)
 235:     # I-bug-946 (Codex iter 2 P2#3 + iter-1 diff P2#2): enforce that the effective
 236:     # entailment model equals the effective evaluator model. Compare EFFECTIVE values
 237:     # (with their defaults) so a single env override that diverges from the default still
 238:     # fails closed — not only the "both env vars set divergently" case.
 239:     _DEFAULT_ENTAILMENT_MODEL = "google/gemma-4-31b-it"  # mirror entailment_judge.py:79
 240:     _DEFAULT_EVALUATOR_MODEL = "google/gemma-4-31b-it"   # mirror pathB_runner.py:37
 241:     eff_entail = (os.environ.get("PG_ENTAILMENT_MODEL") or _DEFAULT_ENTAILMENT_MODEL).strip()
 242:     eff_eval = (os.environ.get("PG_EVALUATOR_MODEL") or _DEFAULT_EVALUATOR_MODEL).strip()
 243:     if eff_entail != eff_eval:
 244:         raise GateError(
 245:             f"effective PG_ENTAILMENT_MODEL={eff_entail!r} != effective PG_EVALUATOR_MODEL"
 246:             f"={eff_eval!r}; the gate cannot pin two different evaluator-family models"
 247:         )
 248:     cfg = build_effective_config(control_vars, salt)
 249:     return {
 250:         "effective_config": cfg,
 251:         "effective_config_hash": effective_config_hash(cfg),
 252:         "control_vars": control_vars,             # the RESOLVED surface (post-run rebuilds from this)
 253:         "control_source_map": source_map or {},   # name -> [file:line, ...] provenance (Codex P2)
 254:         "role_pins": [vars(rp) | {"surrogate_fields": list(rp.surrogate_fields)} for rp in role_pins],
 255:         "reachability_checked": reachability_prober is not None,
 256:         "openrouter_allow_fallbacks": False,
 257:         "openrouter_provider_order": order,
 258:     }

 261: def resolve_role_provider(model_slug: str, provider_order: list[str]) -> str:
 262:     """I-bug-946 (#932): resolve a role's served provider at preflight.
 263: 
 264:     OpenRouter's GET /api/v1/models/<id>/endpoints returns the providers that actually serve
 265:     a model. Smoke #15 demonstrated that without per-role resolution, OpenRouter silently
 266:     routes a role to a provider OUTSIDE the env-pinned order (gemma is not on Fireworks, so
 267:     the evaluator was routed to Novita despite `OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER=fireworks` +
 268:     `allow_fallbacks=false`). The gate caught it correctly; the pin model was wrong.
 269: 
 270:     Algorithm:
 271:       1. Fetch /api/v1/models/<id>/endpoints; parse `data.endpoints`.
 272:       2. Eligible = endpoints with status absent OR status==0. status != 0 means degraded /
 273:          lower-priority per OpenRouter docs (Codex iter-2 P2#4).
 274:       3. Intersect eligible providers (case-insensitive) with `provider_order`.
 275:       4. Return the catalog-cased provider_name of the FIRST match in `provider_order`.
 276:       5. Fail closed with diagnostic if no match OR endpoints list is empty.
 277: 
 278:     Codex APPROVE iter 2 on choice C, brief at .codex/I-bug-946/brief_iter2.md.
 279:     """
 280:     import requests
 281:     api_key = os.environ.get("OPENROUTER_API_KEY")
 282:     headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}"} if api_key else {}
 283:     url = f"https://openrouter.ai/api/v1/models/{model_slug}/endpoints"
 284:     try:
 285:         r = requests.get(url, headers=headers, timeout=20)
 286:         r.raise_for_status()
 287:         endpoints = r.json().get("data", {}).get("endpoints", [])
 288:     except Exception as exc:
 289:         raise GateError(f"OpenRouter endpoints catalog unreachable for {model_slug!r}: {exc}") from exc
 290:     if not endpoints:
 291:         raise GateError(f"OpenRouter has no endpoints for model {model_slug!r} (model offline?)")
 292:     eligible: list[str] = []
 293:     for ep in endpoints:
 294:         status = ep.get("status")
 295:         if status is None or status == 0:
 296:             name = ep.get("provider_name")
 297:             if name:
 298:                 eligible.append(name)
 299:     if not eligible:
 300:         raise GateError(
 301:             f"OpenRouter has no eligible (status==0) endpoints for {model_slug!r}; "
 302:             f"all endpoints degraded"
 303:         )
 304:     eligible_lower = {n.lower(): n for n in eligible}  # case-insensitive lookup, catalog cased value
 305:     for wanted in provider_order:
 306:         catalog_cased = eligible_lower.get(wanted.strip().lower())
 307:         if catalog_cased is not None:
 308:             return catalog_cased
 309:     raise GateError(
 310:         f"OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER={provider_order!r} has no intersection with eligible "
 311:         f"endpoints for {model_slug!r}; available: {sorted(set(eligible))}"
 312:     )
 313:

 317: 
 318:     OpenRouter exposes a list at GET /api/v1/models with `id` (alias) + `canonical_slug`
 319:     (dated snapshot) per entry. The chat-completions response returns `model=<canonical_slug>`
 320:     while the env pin uses `<id>`. Resolving at preflight lets `assert_post_run` accept the
 321:     served canonical_slug without losing pre-registration integrity — the resolved value is
 322:     persisted in `pathB_gate_pin.json` and becomes the audit anchor.
 323: 
 324:     Returns the canonical_slug, or None if it equals model_slug (no dated suffix exposed).
 325:     Raises GateError if the slug is not in the catalog (fail closed) — Codex P2#2.
 326:     """
 327:     import requests
 328:     api_key = os.environ.get("OPENROUTER_API_KEY")
 329:     headers = {"Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}"} if api_key else {}
 330:     try:

  76: def gate_around_question(
  77:     *, enabled: bool, run_dir: Path, control_vars: list[str] | None = None,
  78: ) -> Iterator[None]:
  79:     """Wrap one benchmark question's run with preflight + post-run assertion.
  80: 
  81:     Usage in the runner:
  82:         with gate_around_question(enabled=args.pathB_gate, run_dir=run_dir):
  83:             ... process_query body, including the role-tagged LLM calls ...
  84:             # On normal exit, assert_post_run runs (raises GateError if not full-power).
  85: 
  86:     Behavior:
  87:     - enabled=False: no-op (yields immediately, no capture, no preflight).
  88:     - enabled=True: preflight (raises GateError if not full-power); register_pathB_capture;
  89:       yield; on normal exit, assert_post_run; persist pin + result to ``run_dir``. On
  90:       exception inside the body, capture is cleared but the exception propagates.

  93:         yield
  94:         return

  97:     result_path = run_dir / "pathB_gate_result.json"
  98:     invalid_sentinel = run_dir / "pathB_gate_INVALID"
  99:     run_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
 100: 
 101:     # Codex PR-2 diff iter-1 P3: write a FAIL result file even when preflight raises,
 102:     # so a missing-credential / unreachable-backend failure has an explicit per-run record
 103:     # (otherwise the only artifact is a stderr exception, no traceable artifact).
 104:     try:

 110:             offline=False,  # real run = real reachability ping (gate enforce-by-default).
 111:         )
 112:     except GateError as exc:

 116:                 indent=2, sort_keys=True,

 119:         )
 120:         invalid_sentinel.write_text(
 121:             f"preflight FAIL: {exc}\n", encoding="utf-8",
 122:         )
 123:         logger.error("[pathB] preflight FAIL: %s", exc)
 124:         raise
 125:     pin_path.write_text(json.dumps(pin, indent=2, sort_keys=True, default=str),
 126:                         encoding="utf-8")
 127:     _capture.register_pathB_capture()
 128:     # I-bug-946 (#932): publish the resolved per-role provider mapping via ContextVar so
 129:     # openrouter_client and entailment_judge force singleton routing in their request bodies.
 130:     # Without this, OpenRouter's silent fallback re-routes mid-run and the post_run gate fails
 131:     # (smoke #15: evaluator served by Novita while pin expected Fireworks).
 132:     role_provider_map = {
 133:         rp["role"]: rp["provider_name"]
 134:         for rp in pin.get("role_pins", [])
 135:         if rp.get("provider_name")

 139:         yield
 140:     except Exception:

 142:         if rp_token is not None:
 143:             _capture.reset_role_providers(rp_token)
 144:         _capture.clear_pathB_capture()
 145:         raise

 148:         calls = [LLMCall(**c) for c in _capture.collected_calls()]
 149:         backends = _capture.attempted_backends()
 150:         result = assert_post_run(
 151:             pin=pin,
 152:             control_vars=list(control_vars or []),
 153:             salt=_salt(),
 154:             calls=calls,
 155:             retrieval_backends_attempted=backends,
 156:         )
 157:         result_path.write_text(
 158:             json.dumps({"verdict": "PASS", **result}, indent=2, sort_keys=True, default=str),
 159:             encoding="utf-8",
 160:         )
 161:         logger.info("[pathB] gate PASS for run_dir=%s", run_dir)
 162:     except GateError as exc:
 163:         result_path.write_text(
 164:             json.dumps(
 165:                 {"verdict": "FAIL", "stage": "post_run_assert", "reason": str(exc)},
 166:                 indent=2, sort_keys=True,
 167:             ),
 168:             encoding="utf-8",
 169:         )

 171:         # (PR-3 claim_audit_scorer) can skip the run_dir's per-run artifacts even though
 172:         # they were written during the run (manifest/judge/etc.). The gate is the source
 173:         # of truth for run validity; the sentinel makes that machine-readable.
 174:         invalid_sentinel.write_text(
 175:             f"post-run gate FAIL: {exc}\n", encoding="utf-8",
 176:         )
 177:         logger.error("[pathB] gate FAIL for run_dir=%s: %s", run_dir, exc)
 178:         raise
 179:     finally:
 180:         _capture.clear_pathB_capture()

  82: 
  83: Rules:

  86: - CONTRADICTED: the SENTENCE asserts something the SPAN explicitly disagrees with.

 101:     """Synchronous httpx wrapper around an OpenRouter entailment call.
 102: 
 103:     Lazy-initialized via _get_judge() so import-time cost is zero when
 104:     PG_STRICT_VERIFY_ENTAILMENT=off (the default before I-bug-095).
 105:     """
 106: 
 107:     def __init__(self) -> None:
 108:         import httpx  # local import: avoid forcing the dep when off
 109: 
 110:         # Lazy-import the family-segregation check so the off-mode path
 111:         # never touches openrouter_client. The judge is acting as a
 112:         # content evaluator (Layer-2), so it MUST differ from the
 113:         # generator family per CLAUDE.md §9.1.1 — fail at construction
 114:         # if PG_ENTAILMENT_MODEL is in the same family as PG_GENERATOR_MODEL.
 115:         from src.polaris_graph.llm.openrouter_client import check_family_segregation
 116: 
 117:         api_key = os.environ.get("OPENROUTER_API_KEY", "").strip()
 118:         if not api_key:
 119:             raise RuntimeError(
 120:                 "PG_STRICT_VERIFY_ENTAILMENT requires OPENROUTER_API_KEY"
 121:             )
 122:         self._api_key = api_key
 123:         # I-sov-001: endpoint is env-configurable so the sovereign deploy
 124:         # can point the entailment judge at the OVH H200 vLLM endpoint
 125:         # (set OPENROUTER_BASE_URL=http://<priv-ip>:8000/v1). Default keeps
 126:         # OpenRouter. Mirrors openrouter_client.py:43-45.
 127:         base_url = os.environ.get(
 128:             "OPENROUTER_BASE_URL", "https://openrouter.ai/api/v1"
 129:         ).rstrip("/")
 130:         self._endpoint = f"{base_url}/chat/completions"
 131:         self._model = os.environ.get(
 132:             "PG_ENTAILMENT_MODEL", _DEFAULT_ENTAILMENT_MODEL
 133:         )
 134:         # Two-family invariant per §9.1.1: raises RuntimeError if the
 135:         # entailment judge ends up in the same family as the generator
 136:         # (e.g. an operator setting PG_ENTAILMENT_MODEL to a DeepSeek
 137:         # variant when PG_GENERATOR_MODEL is also DeepSeek). The
 138:         # default model (google/gemma-4-31b-it) is in a different
 139:         # family from DeepSeek by construction.
 140:         check_family_segregation(evaluator_model=self._model)
 141:         self._client = httpx.Client(timeout=_ENTAILMENT_TIMEOUT_S)
 142: 
 143:     def judge(self, sentence: str, span: str) -> tuple[str, str]:
 144:         """Return (verdict, reason).
 145: 
 146:         verdict is one of "ENTAILED", "NEUTRAL", "CONTRADICTED".
 147:         On API/parse failure returns ("ENTAILED", "judge_error: ...") —
 148:         fail-open so a transient OpenRouter outage does not nuke a run.
 149: 
 150:         I-bug-100: after each successful httpx call this method records
 151:         the call cost via openrouter_client's module-level helpers
 152:         (`_add_run_cost`, `check_run_budget`, `_COST_LEDGER_PATH`) so
 153:         judge spend is visible to the per-run budget cap and the cost
 154:         ledger. `BudgetExceededError` is explicitly re-raised before
 155:         the broad `except Exception` fail-open handler so a cap breach
 156:         aborts the sweep cleanly instead of being masked as a transient
 157:         judge error.
 158:         """
 159:         prompt = _ENTAILMENT_PROMPT.format(span=span, sentence=sentence)
 160:         started = time.monotonic()
 161:         # I-bug-946 (#932): when Path-B gate is active, force singleton provider routing in
 162:         # the request body to match the resolved-at-preflight per-role provider. Without this,
 163:         # this direct httpx path bypasses the gate's routing intent (the OpenRouterClient path
 164:         # also got the override via openrouter_client.py:1400-1410). Codex iter-2 P1#2.
 165:         # Codex iter-1 diff P1#2: this lookup MUST use explicit role="evaluator", NOT the
 166:         # ambient _ROLE contextvar. The entailment judge fires during section generation
 167:         # (where _ROLE=="generator"), but it posts the evaluator-family model — using the
 168:         # ambient role would route Gemma to the generator's provider (Fireworks, no Gemma).
 169:         try:
 170:             from src.polaris_graph.benchmark import pathB_capture as _pathb_for_routing
 171:             _gate_provider = _pathb_for_routing.get_role_provider("evaluator")
 172:         except Exception:
 173:             _gate_provider = None
 174:         json_body: dict = {
 175:             "model": self._model,
 176:             "messages": [{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
 177:             "temperature": 0.0,
 178:             "max_tokens": 100,
 179:             "response_format": {"type": "json_object"},
 180:         }
 181:         if _gate_provider:
 182:             json_body["provider"] = {
 183:                 "order": [_gate_provider],
 184:                 "allow_fallbacks": False,
 185:                 "require_parameters": True,
 186:             }
 187:         try:
 188:             response = self._client.post(
 189:                 self._endpoint,
 190:                 headers={
 191:                     "Authorization": f"Bearer {self._api_key}",
 192:                     "Content-Type": "application/json",
 193:                 },
 194:                 json=json_body,
 195:             )
 196:             response.raise_for_status()
 197:             data = response.json()
 198: 
 199:             # I-safety-002b (#925): Path-B gate capture. The entailment judge is the
 200:             # evaluator-family LLM call that bypasses OpenRouterClient (direct httpx),
 201:             # so without capturing here the gate's two-family completeness check would
 202:             # be a silent no-op. Best-effort + gate-flagged; lazy import keeps off-mode
 203:             # import cost zero. `data` is the genuinely-served non-stream JSON.
 204:             try:
 205:                 from src.polaris_graph.benchmark import pathB_capture as _pathb
 206:                 if _pathb.is_active():
 207:                     _pathb.capture_llm_call(
 208:                         role="evaluator",
 209:                         messages=[{"role": "user", "content": prompt}],
 210:                         raw_response=data,
 211:                     )
 212:             except Exception:  # noqa: BLE001 — capture must never break the judge
 213:                 pass
 214: 
 215:             # I-bug-100: cost recording. Reads + records BEFORE verdict
 216:             # parse so a cap breach aborts the sweep regardless of
 217:             # downstream parse outcome.
 218:             usage = data.get("usage", {}) or {}
 219:             input_tokens = int(usage.get("prompt_tokens", 0) or 0)
 220:             output_tokens = int(usage.get("completion_tokens", 0) or 0)
 221:             api_cost = float(usage.get("cost", 0) or 0)
 222:             actual_cost = api_cost or _orc._impute_cost_from_tokens(
 223:                 self._model, input_tokens, output_tokens, 0,
 224:             )
 225:             # I-bug-100 iter-1 diff P2 fix: when the entire usage block
 226:             # is absent, both api_cost and the imputed value are 0, which
 227:             # silently bypasses the budget guard. Fall back to a
 228:             # conservative estimate based on typical judge-call shape
 229:             # (~500 prompt + ~100 completion tokens) priced at Opus-tier
 230:             # so the budget cap is preserved on degraded responses.

 376: def assert_post_run(

 378:     control_vars: list[str],

 382: ) -> dict:
 383:     """Fatal post-run gate (Codex). Any violation ⇒ run INVALID, discard + re-run.
 384: 
 385:     Returns the established per-role served-identity surrogates on success."""
 386:     # config no-drift — rebuild from the SAME resolved surface preflight pinned (not a
 387:     # caller-passed list, which could differ / bypass; Codex iter-2).

 391:         raise GateError("effective_config drifted between preflight and post-run")
 392:     pins_by_role = {rp["role"]: rp for rp in pin["role_pins"]}

 394:         raise GateError("no LLM calls captured — completeness check cannot pass")

 396:     roles_seen = {c.role for c in calls}
 397:     missing_roles = set(pins_by_role) - roles_seen
 398:     if missing_roles:
 399:         raise GateError(f"completeness: pinned role(s) with no captured LLM call: {missing_roles}")
 400:     surrogate_by_role: dict[str, set[str]] = {}
 401:     for c in calls:
 402:         if not (c.prompt_messages_present and c.request_hash and c.response_metadata):
 403:             raise GateError(f"call {c.call_id}: incomplete capture (prompt/request_hash/metadata)")
 404:         rp = pins_by_role.get(c.role)
 405:         if rp is None:
 406:             raise GateError(f"call {c.call_id}: role {c.role!r} not pinned")

 409:                 raise GateError(f"call {c.call_id}: served metadata missing surrogate field {fld!r}")
 410:         # EXACT provider + EXACT full-slug model match (Codex P1 — no loose substring).
 411:         # I-bug-944 (#925 smoke #13): provider comparison is case-insensitive (OpenRouter
 412:         # returns "Fireworks" / "DeepInfra" with title case while the pin env var
 413:         # OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER is documented lower-case; case-mismatch is identity-

 415:         # case-sensitive — slugs are canonical.
 416:         served_provider = (c.response_metadata.get("provider_name") or "").strip().lower()

 418:         if served_provider != pinned_provider:

 436:         normalized_metadata = dict(c.response_metadata)

 440:     for role, ids in surrogate_by_role.items():

 442:             raise GateError(f"role {role}: served-identity surrogate drifted across calls ({len(ids)} distinct)")

 155:     sink = _SINK.get()

 159: def request_hash(messages) -> str:
 160:     """Stable hash of the prompt messages (presence/integrity, not content storage)."""
 161:     try:
 162:         payload = json.dumps(messages, sort_keys=True, ensure_ascii=False, default=str)
 163:     except (TypeError, ValueError):
 164:         payload = repr(messages)
 165:     return hashlib.sha256(payload.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
 166: 
 167: 
 168: def build_response_metadata(raw_response: dict | None) -> dict:
 169:     """Served-identity metadata from the provider response — PROVEN-present fields only.
 170: 
 171:     provider_name <- raw['provider'] (OpenRouter), model <- served raw['model'],
 172:     system_fingerprint <- raw['system_fingerprint']. None/missing fields are DROPPED
 173:     (never request-filled), so an unreported served provider/model surfaces as a gate
 174:     failure rather than a false pass.
 175: 
 176:     Streaming responses synthesize ``data`` with a request-derived ``model`` fallback, so
 177:     the client stashes the genuinely-SSE-served identity under ``_pathb_served``; when that
 178:     key is present it is the authoritative source (request-derived ``data['model']`` is
 179:     never counted as served)."""
 180:     raw = raw_response or {}
 181:     served = raw.get("_pathb_served")
 182:     src = served if isinstance(served, dict) else raw
 183:     meta = {
 184:         "provider_name": src.get("provider"),
 185:         "model": src.get("model"),
 186:         "system_fingerprint": src.get("system_fingerprint"),
 187:     }
 188:     return {k: v for k, v in meta.items() if v is not None}
 189: 
 190: 
 191: def capture_llm_call(*, role: str, messages, raw_response: dict | None) -> None:
 192:     """Best-effort: append one captured provider completion. Never raises; no-op when off."""
 193:     sink = _SINK.get()
 194:     if sink is None:
 195:         return
 196:     try:
 197:         sink.append(
 198:             {
 199:                 "call_id": f"{role}-{len(sink)}",
 200:                 "role": role,
 201:                 "prompt_messages_present": bool(messages),
 202:                 "request_hash": request_hash(messages),
 203:                 "response_metadata": build_response_metadata(raw_response),
 204:             }
 205:         )
 206:     except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 — capture must never break generation
 207:         logger.warning("[pathB] capture_llm_call failed (%s) — call not recorded", exc)

import os
from scripts.dr_benchmark.pathB_run_gate import preflight, RolePin
import requests

class R:
    def __init__(self, payload): self._payload = payload
    def raise_for_status(self): pass
    def json(self): return self._payload

def mock_get(url, *args, **kwargs):
    if url.endswith('/models'):
        return R({'data': [
            {'id': 'deepseek/deepseek-v4-pro', 'canonical_slug': 'deepseek/deepseek-v4-pro-x'},
            {'id': 'google/gemma-4-31b-it', 'canonical_slug': 'google/gemma-4-31b-it-y'},
        ]})
    if 'deepseek-v4-pro' in url:
        return R({'data': {'endpoints': [{'provider_name': 'Fireworks', 'status': 0}]}})
    if 'gemma-4-31b-it' in url:
        return R({'data': {'endpoints': [{'provider_name': 'Novita', 'status': 0}]}})
    raise AssertionError(url)

old_get = requests.get
requests.get = mock_get
try:
    os.environ['OPENROUTER_ALLOW_FALLBACKS'] = 'false'
    os.environ['OPENROUTER_PROVIDER_ORDER'] = 'fireworks,novita'
    os.environ['SERPER_API_KEY'] = 'x'
    os.environ['SEMANTIC_SCHOLAR_API_KEY'] = 'y'

        RolePin('generator', 'deepseek/deepseek-v4-pro', 'WRONG', ('provider_name','model')),
        RolePin('evaluator', 'google/gemma-4-31b-it', 'WRONG', ('provider_name','model')),
    ]
    pin = preflight([], pins, b'salt', offline=False, reachability_prober=lambda b: True)
    print({rp['role']: rp['provider_name'] for rp in pin['role_pins']})
finally:
    requests.get = old_get

 309: # I-bug-096: process-lifetime telemetry counters for the entailment gate.
 310: # In enforce mode the judge fail-open path returns ("ENTAILED",
 311: # "judge_error: ...") on transient API errors. A persistent OpenRouter
 312: # outage or model-format change could make the 6th check silently inert
 313: # — every sentence falls through as ENTAILED while WARNING lines
 314: # accumulate. These counters give an operator a concise "the gate ran N
 315: # times, M of those errored" signal.
 316: #
 317: # Counters are gate-side (not judge-side) per the original I-bug-092
 318: # brief verdict: gate behavior is what we want to measure, not a
 319: # specific judge implementation. Tests with FakeJudge tick these too,
 320: # and a future swapped judge cannot bypass the judge_error counter.
